This is the API description for the WalcuCRM service

Terms of service
Contact Walcu API Support
Servers

https://api.crm.walcu.com/dealers/{dealer_id} - Base URL for the API
Computed URL:https://api.crm.walcu.com/dealers/
Server variables
dealer_id
Authorize
